    INNER JOIN "CLIENTE" AS c ON f."ID_CLIENTE" = c."ID_CLIENTE"
    WHERE f."ID_FACTURA" = @__idFactura_0
    LIMIT 1
) AS t
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT a."ID_ARTICULO_FACTURA", a."CANTIDAD", a."CODIGO", a."DESCRIPCION", a."DESCUENTO", a."ID_ARTICULO", a."ID_FACTURA", a."PRECIO_UNITARIO", a0."ID_ARTICULO" AS "ID_ARTICULO0", a0."CODIGO" AS "CODIGO0", a0."DESCRIPCION" AS "DESCRIPCION0", a0."HABILITADO", a0."ID_ARTICULO_PRECIO", a0."ID_ASOCIADO_RELLENO", a0."ID_COLOR", a0."ID_FABRICANTE", a0."ID_MEDIDA", a0."ID_SUBFAMILIA", a0."STOCK", c0."ID_COLOR" AS "ID_COLOR0", c0."CODIGO" AS "CODIGO1", c0."HEXA", c0."DESCRIPCION" AS "DESCRIPCION1", m."ID_MEDIDA" AS "ID_MEDIDA0", m."CODIGO" AS "CODIGO2", m."DESCRIPCION" AS "DESCRIPCION2", a1."ID_ARTICULO_PRECIO" AS "ID_ARTICULO_PRECIO0", a1."CODIGO" AS "CODIGO3", a1."DESCRIPCION" AS "DESCRIPCION3", a1."PRECIO1", a1."PRECIO2", a1."PRECIO3", a1."RELLENO", s."ID_SUBFAMILIA" AS "ID_SUBFAMILIA0", s."CODIGO" AS "CODIGO4", s."DESCRIPCION" AS "DESCRIPCION4"
    FROM "ARTICULO_FACTURA" AS a
    INNER JOIN "ARTICULO" AS a0 ON a."ID_ARTICULO" = a0."ID_ARTICULO"
    INNER JOIN "COLOR" AS c0 ON a0."ID_COLOR" = c0."ID_COLOR"
    INNER JOIN "MEDIDA" AS m ON a0."ID_MEDIDA" = m."ID_MEDIDA"
    LEFT JOIN "ARTICULO_PRECIO" AS a1 ON a0."ID_ARTICULO_PRECIO" = a1."ID_ARTICULO_PRECIO"
    LEFT JOIN "SUBFAMILIA" AS s ON a0."ID_SUBFAMILIA" = s."ID_SUBFAMILIA"
) AS t0 ON t."ID_FACTURA" = t0."ID_FACTURA"
ORDER BY t."ID_FACTURA", t."ID_CLIENTE0", t0."ID_ARTICULO_FACTURA", t0."ID_ARTICULO0", t0."ID_COLOR0", t0."ID_MEDIDA0", t0."ID_ARTICULO_PRECIO0"
